<div class="form-popup" id="formPopup"><h3 id="formTitle">Форма</h3><div id="formContent"></div><button onclick="closeForm()">Закрыть</button></div>

<script>
    let currentUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('library_user')) || null;
    let users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('library_users')) || [];
    let books = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('library_books')) || [];
    let loans = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('library_loans')) || [];

    function saveData() {
        localStorage.setItem('library_users', JSON.stringify(users));
        localStorage.setItem('library_books', JSON.stringify(books));
        localStorage.setItem('library_loans', JSON.stringify(loans));
    }

    function showMessage(text, type) {
        let msg = document.createElement('div');
        msg.className = `message ${type}`;
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
        document.body.appendChild(msg);
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 3000);
    }

    function render() {
        const authContainer = document.getElementById('authContainer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('mainContent');
        const authButtons = document.getElementById('authButtons');
        if (currentUser) {
            authContainer.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('userName').textContent = currentUser.fullName || currentUser.login;
            document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = currentUser.role === 'reader' ? 'Читатель' : (currentUser.role === 'librarian' ? 'Библиотекарь' : 'Администратор');
            authButtons.innerHTML = `<button class="logout-btn" onclick="logout()">Выйти</button>`;
            renderCards();
        } else {
            authContainer.style.display = 'block';
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            authButtons.innerHTML = '';
            showAuthForm();
        }
    }

    function showAuthForm() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>📚 Библиотека</h2>
            <div id="loginForm">
                <input type="text" id="loginUsername" placeholder="Логин"><input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <button onclick="login()">Войти</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showRegister()">Нет аккаунта? Зарегистрироваться</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function showRegister() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>Регистрация</h2>
            <div id="registerForm">
                <input type="text" id="regFullName" placeholder="ФИО"><input type="text" id="regLogin" placeholder="Логин">
                <input type="password" id="regPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <select id="regRole"><option value="reader">Читатель</option><option value="librarian">Библиотекарь</option><option value="admin">Администратор</option></select>
                <button onclick="register()">Зарегистрироваться</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showAuthForm()">Уже есть аккаунт? Войти</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function register() {
        const fullName = document.getElementById('regFullName')?.value;
        const login = document.getElementById('regLogin')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('regPassword')?.value;
        const role = document.getElementById('regRole')?.value;
        if (!fullName || !login || !password) { showMessage('Заполните все поля', 'error'); return; }
        if (users.find(u => u.login === login)) { showMessage('Пользователь существует', 'error'); return; }
        users.push({ id: Date.now(), fullName, login, password, role });
        saveData();
        showMessage('Регистрация успешна!', 'success');
        showAuthForm();
    }

    function login() {
        const login = document.getElementById('loginUsername')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword')?.value;
        const user = users.find(u => u.login === login && u.password === password);
        if (user) { currentUser = user; localStorage.setItem('library_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser)); render(); }
        else { showMessage('Неверный логин или пароль', 'error'); }
    }

    function logout() { currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('library_user'); render(); }

    if (books.length === 0) {
        books = [
            { id: 1, title: "Мастер и Маргарита", author: "Булгаков М.", year: 1967, copies: 3, available: 3 },
            { id: 2, title: "Преступление и наказание", author: "Достоевский Ф.", year: 1866, copies: 2, available: 2 },
            { id: 3, title: "Война и мир", author: "Толстой Л.", year: 1869, copies: 4, available: 4 },
            { id: 4, title: "Евгений Онегин", author: "Пушкин А.", year: 1833, copies: 3, available: 3 }
        ];
        saveData();
    }

    function renderCards() {
        const container = document.getElementById('cardsContainer');
        if (currentUser.role === 'reader') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>🔍 Поиск книг</h3><p>Найдите книгу в каталоге</p><button onclick="searchBooks()">Искать</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📖 Мои книги</h3><p>Взятые книги и задолженности</p><button onclick="showMyLoans()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>⭐ Рекомендации</h3><p>Популярные книги</p><button onclick="showRecommendations()">Смотреть</button></div>`;
        } else if (currentUser.role === 'librarian') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📋 Выдача книг</h3><p>Оформление выдачи</p><button onclick="showIssueForm()">Выдать</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📥 Возврат книг</h3><p>Оформление возврата</p><button onclick="showReturnForm()">Принять</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📊 Отчет по выдаче</h3><p>Статистика</p><button onclick="showReport()">Сформировать</button></div>`;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = `<div class="card"><h3>📚 Добавить книгу</h3><p>Пополнение фонда</p><button onclick="addBookForm()">Добавить</button></div>`;
        }
    }

    function searchBooks() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Поиск книг';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <input id="searchInput" placeholder="Введите название или автора">
            <button onclick="doSearch()">Найти</button>
            <div id="searchResults"></div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function doSearch() {
        const query = document.getElementById('searchInput')?.value.toLowerCase();
        const results = books.filter(b => b.title.toLowerCase().includes(query) || b.author.toLowerCase().includes(query));
        const resultsDiv = document.getElementById('searchResults');
        if (results.length === 0) { resultsDiv.innerHTML = '<p>Ничего не найдено</p>'; }
        else {
            resultsDiv.innerHTML = results.map(b => `<div class="book-card"><strong>${b.title}</strong><br>${b.author}, ${b.year}<br>Доступно: ${b.available} из ${b.copies}<br>${b.available > 0 ? `<button onclick="borrowBook(${b.id})">Взять книгу</button>` : '<span class="fine">Нет в наличии</span>'}</div>`).join('');
        }
    }

    function borrowBook(id) {
        const book = books.find(b => b.id === id);
        if (book && book.available > 0) {
            book.available--;
            const dueDate = new Date();
            dueDate.setDate(dueDate.getDate() + 14);
            loans.push({ id: Date.now(), bookId: id, bookTitle: book.title, userId: currentUser.id, userName: currentUser.fullName, borrowDate: new Date().toLocaleString(), dueDate: dueDate.toLocaleDateString(), returned: false });
            saveData();
            showMessage(`Книга "${book.title}" выдана! Срок возврата: ${dueDate.toLocaleDateString()}`, 'success');
            doSearch();
        }
    }

    function showMyLoans() {
        const myLoans = loans.filter(l => l.userId === currentUser.id && !l.returned);
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мои книги';
        if (myLoans.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>У вас нет взятых книг</p>'; }
        else {
            document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${myLoans.map(l => `<div class="book-card"><strong>${l.bookTitle}</strong><br>Взята: ${l.borrowDate}<br>Вернуть до: ${l.dueDate}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        }
        openForm();
    }

    function showRecommendations() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Популярные книги';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${books.map(b => `<div class="book-card"><strong>${b.title}</strong> - ${b.author}<br>В наличии: ${b.available} экз.</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function showIssueForm() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Выдача книги';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <input id="readerName" placeholder="ФИО читателя"><select id="bookSelect"><option>Выберите книгу</option>${books.filter(b=>b.available>0).map(b=>`<option value="${b.id}">${b.title}</option>`).join('')}</select>
            <button onclick="issueBook()">Выдать</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function issueBook() {
        const readerName = document.getElementById('readerName')?.value;
        const bookId = document.getElementById('bookSelect')?.value;
        if (!readerName || !bookId) { showMessage('Заполните поля', 'error'); return; }
        const book = books.find(b => b.id == bookId);
        if (book && book.available > 0) {
            book.available--;
            const dueDate = new Date();
            dueDate.setDate(dueDate.getDate() + 14);
            loans.push({ id: Date.now(), bookId: book.id, bookTitle: book.title, userId: Date.now(), userName: readerName, borrowDate: new Date().toLocaleString(), dueDate: dueDate.toLocaleDateString(), returned: false });
            saveData();
            showMessage(`Книга "${book.title}" выдана ${readerName}`, 'success');
            closeForm();
        }
    }

    function showReturnForm() {
        const activeLoans = loans.filter(l => !l.returned);
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Возврат книги';
        if (activeLoans.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет выданных книг</p>'; }
        else {
            document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select id="returnSelect"><option>Выберите книгу</option>${activeLoans.map(l => `<option value="${l.id}">${l.bookTitle} - ${l.userName}</option>`).join('')}</select><button onclick="returnBook()">Принять возврат</button>`;
        }
        openForm();
    }

    function returnBook() {
        const loanId = document.getElementById('returnSelect')?.value;
        if (!loanId) { showMessage('Выберите книгу', 'error'); return; }
        const loan = loans.find(l => l.id == loanId);
        if (loan) {
            loan.returned = true;
            const book = books.find(b => b.id === loan.bookId);
            if (book) book.available++;
            saveData();
            showMessage(`Книга "${loan.bookTitle}" возвращена`, 'success');
            closeForm();
        }
    }

    function showReport() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отчет'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="book-card">Выдано книг: ${loans.filter(l=>!l.returned).length}<br>Всего книг в фонде: ${books.reduce((s,b)=>s+b.copies,0)}</div>`; openForm(); }
    function addBookForm() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Добавление книги'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<input id="title" placeholder="Название"><input id="author" placeholder="Автор"><input id="year" placeholder="Год"><input id="copies" placeholder="Количество экземпляров"><button onclick="addBook()">Добавить</button>`; openForm(); }
    function addBook() {
        const title = document.getElementById('title')?.value;
        if (!title) { showMessage('Введите название', 'error'); return; }
        const copies = parseInt(document.getElementById('copies')?.value) || 1;
        books.push({ id: Date.now(), title, author: document.getElementById('author')?.value, year: document.getElementById('year')?.value, copies: copies, available: copies });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage('Книга добавлена', 'success');
    }

    function openForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'block'; }
    function closeForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'none'; }

    if (users.length === 0) {
        users = [{ id: 1, fullName: "Читатель", login: "reader", password: "123", role: "reader" },
                 { id: 2, fullName: "Библиотекарь", login: "librarian", password: "123", role: "librarian" },
                 { id: 3, fullName: "Админ", login: "admin", password: "123", role: "admin" }];
        saveData();
    }
    render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
<div class="container">
    <div class="header">
        <div class="logo"><h1>💅 Салон красоты</h1><p>Студия красоты</p></div>
        <div class="auth-buttons" id="authButtons"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="mainContent" class="main-content">
        <div class="welcome-section"><h2>Добро пожаловать, <span id="userName"></span>!</h2><p>Роль: <strong id="userRole"></strong></p></div>
        <div class="cards" id="cardsContainer"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="authContainer" class="auth-container"></div>

<div class="overlay" id="overlay"></div>
<div class="form-popup" id="formPopup"><h3 id="formTitle">Форма</h3><div id="formContent"></div><button onclick="closeForm()">Закрыть</button></div>

<script>
    let currentUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('beauty_user')) || null;
    let users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('beauty_users')) || [];
    let appointments = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('beauty_appointments')) || [];

    const services = [
        { id: 1, name: "Стрижка", price: 1500, duration: 60 },
        { id: 2, name: "Окрашивание", price: 3500, duration: 120 },
        { id: 3, name: "Маникюр", price: 1200, duration: 60 },
        { id: 4, name: "Педикюр", price: 1800, duration: 60 },
        { id: 5, name: "Укладка", price: 1000, duration: 45 }
    ];

    const masters = [
        { id: 1, name: "Анна", specialty: "Парикмахер", rating: 4.8 },
        { id: 2, name: "Елена", specialty: "Маникюр", rating: 4.9 },
        { id: 3, name: "Мария", specialty: "Универсал", rating: 4.7 }
    ];

    function saveData() {
        localStorage.setItem('beauty_users', JSON.stringify(users));
        localStorage.setItem('beauty_appointments', JSON.stringify(appointments));
    }

    function showMessage(text, type) {
        let msg = document.createElement('div');
        msg.className = `message ${type}`;
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
        document.body.appendChild(msg);
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 3000);
    }

    function render() {
        const authContainer = document.getElementById('authContainer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('mainContent');
        const authButtons = document.getElementById('authButtons');
        if (currentUser) {
            authContainer.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('userName').textContent = currentUser.fullName || currentUser.login;
            document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = currentUser.role === 'client' ? 'Клиент' : (currentUser.role === 'admin' ? 'Администратор' : 'Мастер');
            authButtons.innerHTML = `<button class="logout-btn" onclick="logout()">Выйти</button>`;
            renderCards();
        } else {
            authContainer.style.display = 'block';
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            authButtons.innerHTML = '';
            showAuthForm();
        }
    }

    function showAuthForm() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>💅 Салон красоты</h2>
            <div id="loginForm">
                <input type="text" id="loginUsername" placeholder="Логин"><input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <button onclick="login()">Войти</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showRegister()">Нет аккаунта? Зарегистрироваться</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function showRegister() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>Регистрация</h2>
            <div id="registerForm">
                <input type="text" id="regFullName" placeholder="ФИО"><input type="text" id="regLogin" placeholder="Логин">
                <input type="password" id="regPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <select id="regRole"><option value="client">Клиент</option><option value="admin">Администратор</option><option value="master">Мастер</option></select>
                <button onclick="register()">Зарегистрироваться</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showAuthForm()">Уже есть аккаунт? Войти</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function register() {
        const fullName = document.getElementById('regFullName')?.value;
        const login = document.getElementById('regLogin')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('regPassword')?.value;
        const role = document.getElementById('regRole')?.value;
        if (!fullName || !login || !password) { showMessage('Заполните все поля', 'error'); return; }
        if (users.find(u => u.login === login)) { showMessage('Пользователь существует', 'error'); return; }
        users.push({ id: Date.now(), fullName, login, password, role });
        saveData();
        showMessage('Регистрация успешна!', 'success');
        showAuthForm();
    }

    function login() {
        const login = document.getElementById('loginUsername')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword')?.value;
        const user = users.find(u => u.login === login && u.password === password);
        if (user) { currentUser = user; localStorage.setItem('beauty_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser)); render(); }
        else { showMessage('Неверный логин или пароль', 'error'); }
    }

    function logout() { currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('beauty_user'); render(); }

    function renderCards() {
        const container = document.getElementById('cardsContainer');
        if (currentUser.role === 'client') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>✂️ Услуги</h3><p>Выберите услугу</p><button onclick="showServices()">Выбрать</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📅 Мои записи</h3><p>Просмотр записей</p><button onclick="showMyAppointments()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>⭐ Отзывы</h3><p>Оставить отзыв о мастере</p><button onclick="leaveReview()">Оставить</button></div>`;
        } else if (currentUser.role === 'admin') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📅 Расписание</h3><p>Управление записями</p><button onclick="showSchedule()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>💰 Отчет по выручке</h3><p>Финансы</p><button onclick="showRevenue()">Сформировать</button></div>`;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📋 Мои записи</h3><p>Расписание мастера</p><button onclick="showMasterSchedule()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>✅ Отметить выполнение</h3><p>Завершить услугу</p><button onclick="completeService()">Отметить</button></div>`;
        }
    }

    function showServices() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Услуги';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${services.map(s => `<div class="service-card"><div><strong>${s.name}</strong><br>${s.price} руб | ${s.duration} мин</div><button onclick="selectService(${s.id})">Выбрать</button></div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function selectService(serviceId) {
        const service = services.find(s => s.id === serviceId);
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <h3>Вы выбрали: ${service.name}</h3>
            <p>Стоимость: ${service.price} руб</p>
            <p>Выберите мастера:</p>
            <div>${masters.map(m => `<div class="master-card" onclick="selectMaster(${m.id}, ${serviceId})">${m.name}<br>⭐ ${m.rating}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
    }

    function selectMaster(masterId, serviceId) {
        const service = services.find(s => s.id === serviceId);
        const master = masters.find(m => m.id === masterId);
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <p>Запись к ${master.name} на ${service.name}</p>
            <input type="date" id="date"><input type="time" id="time">
            <button onclick="bookAppointment(${masterId}, ${serviceId})">Записаться</button>`;
    }

    function bookAppointment(masterId, serviceId) {
        const date = document.getElementById('date')?.value;
        const time = document.getElementById('time')?.value;
        if (!date || !time) { showMessage('Выберите дату и время', 'error'); return; }
        const service = services.find(s => s.id === serviceId);
        const master = masters.find(m => m.id === masterId);
        appointments.push({ id: Date.now(), clientId: currentUser.id, clientName: currentUser.fullName, masterId, masterName: master.name, serviceId, serviceName: service.name, price: service.price, date, time, status: 'Записан' });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage(`Вы записаны к ${master.name} на ${date} ${time}`, 'success');
    }

    function showMyAppointments() {
        const myAppointments = appointments.filter(a => a.clientId === currentUser.id);
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мои записи';
        if (myAppointments.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет записей</p>'; }
        else { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${myAppointments.map(a => `<div class="service-card">${a.serviceName} - ${a.masterName}<br>${a.date} ${a.time}<br>Статус: ${a.status}</div>`).join('')}</div>`; }
        openForm();
    }

    function leaveReview() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отзыв'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select><option>Выберите мастера</option>${masters.map(m=>`<option>${m.name}</option>`).join('')}</select><textarea placeholder="Ваш отзыв"></textarea><button onclick="showMessage('Спасибо за отзыв!','success');closeForm()">Отправить</button>`; openForm(); }
    function showSchedule() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Расписание'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="service-card">Сегодня: 5 записей<br>Завтра: 3 записи</div>`; openForm(); }
    function showRevenue() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Выручка'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="service-card">Выручка за месяц: 150 000 руб</div>`; openForm(); }
    function showMasterSchedule() { const myAppointments = appointments.filter(a => a.masterName === currentUser.fullName); document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мое расписание'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = myAppointments.length ? `<div>${myAppointments.map(a=>`<div class="service-card">${a.serviceName} - ${a.clientName}<br>${a.date} ${a.time}</div>`).join('')}</div>` : '<p>Нет записей</p>'; openForm(); }
    function completeService() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Выполнение'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select><option>Выберите запись</option></select><button onclick="showMessage('Услуга выполнена','success');closeForm()">Отметить</button>`; openForm(); }

    function openForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'block'; }
    function closeForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'none'; }

    if (users.length === 0) {
        users = [{ id: 1, fullName: "Клиент", login: "client", password: "123", role: "client" },
                 { id: 2, fullName: "Админ", login: "admin", password: "123", role: "admin" },
                 { id: 3, fullName: "Анна", login: "master", password: "123", role: "master" }];
        saveData();
    }
    render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

Вариант 18: Компания по грузоперевозкам
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="ru">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Грузоперевозки - Транспортная компания</title>
    <style>
        * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }
        body {
            font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #2980b9 0%, #1a5276 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
            padding: 20px;
        }
        .container {
            max-width: 1200px;
            width: 100%;
            background: white;
            border-radius: 20px;
            overflow: hidden;
            box-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
        }
        .header {
            background: #1a5276;
            color: white;
            padding: 20px 30px;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .logo h1 { font-size: 1.5rem; }
        .auth-buttons button {
            background: #e74c3c;

            border-radius: 8px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .auth-buttons .logout-btn { background: #7f8c8d; }
        .main-content { padding: 30px; display: none; }
        .cards {
            display: grid;
            grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr));
            gap: 20px;
            margin-top: 20px;
        }
        .card {
            background: #f8f9fa;
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 15px;
            border-left: 4px solid #2980b9;

        .card button {
            background: #2980b9;

            border-radius: 5px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .form-popup {
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            top: 50%;

            background: white;
            padding: 30px;
            border-radius: 15px;
            width: 400px;
            max-height: 80vh;
            overflow-y: auto;
            z-index: 1000;
        }
        .form-popup input, .form-popup select, .form-popup textarea {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 10px;
            margin: 10px 0;
            border: 1px solid #ddd;
            border-radius: 5px;
        }
        .form-popup button {
            background: #2ecc71;
            color: white;
            border: none;
            padding: 10px;
            width: 100%;
            border-radius: 5px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .overlay {
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100%;
            height: 100%;
            background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5);
            z-index: 999;
        }
        .auth-container { padding: 40px; text-align: center; }
        .auth-container input {
            width: 100%;
            max-width: 300px;
            padding: 12px;
            margin: 10px auto;
            border: 1px solid #ddd;
            border-radius: 8px;
            display: block;
        }
        .auth-container button {
            background: #1a5276;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px 30px;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 8px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .toggle-auth { color: #2980b9; cursor: pointer; margin-top: 15px; display: inline-block; }
        .message {
            padding: 10px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            right: 20px;
            z-index: 2000;
            display: none;
        }
        .success { background: #d4edda; color: #155724; }
        .error { background: #f8d7da; color: #721c24; }
        .cargo-card {
            background: #f8f9fa;
            padding: 12px;
            margin-bottom: 10px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            border-left: 3px solid #2980b9;
        }
        .track-status {
            display: inline-block;
            padding: 3px 10px;
            border-radius: 15px;
            font-size: 11px;
        }
        .status-new { background: #f39c12; color: white; }
        .status-transit { background: #3498db; color: white; }
        .status-delivered { background: #2ecc71; color: white; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <div class="header">
        <div class="logo"><h1>🚚 Грузоперевозки</h1><p>Транспортная компания</p></div>
        <div class="auth-buttons" id="authButtons"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="mainContent" class="main-content">
        <div class="welcome-section"><h2>Добро пожаловать, <span id="userName"></span>!</h2><p>Роль: <strong id="userRole"></strong></p></div>
        <div class="cards" id="cardsContainer"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="authContainer" class="auth-container"></div>
</div>
<div class="overlay" id="overlay"></div>
<div class="form-popup" id="formPopup"><h3 id="formTitle">Форма</h3><div id="formContent"></div><button onclick="closeForm()">Закрыть</button></div>

<script>
    let currentUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cargo_user')) || null;
    let users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cargo_users')) || [];
    let shipments = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cargo_shipments')) || [];

    function saveData() {
        localStorage.setItem('cargo_users', JSON.stringify(users));
        localStorage.setItem('cargo_shipments', JSON.stringify(shipments));
    }

    function showMessage(text, type) {
        let msg = document.createElement('div');
        msg.className = `message ${type}`;
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
        document.body.appendChild(msg);
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 3000);
    }

    function render() {
        const authContainer = document.getElementById('authContainer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('mainContent');
        const authButtons = document.getElementById('authButtons');
        if (currentUser) {
            authContainer.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('userName').textContent = currentUser.fullName || currentUser.login;
            document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = currentUser.role === 'client' ? 'Клиент' : (currentUser.role === 'logist' ? 'Логист' : 'Водитель');
            authButtons.innerHTML = `<button class="logout-btn" onclick="logout()">Выйти</button>`;
            renderCards();
        } else {
            authContainer.style.display = 'block';
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            authButtons.innerHTML = '';
            showAuthForm();
        }
    }

    function showAuthForm() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>🚚 Грузоперевозки</h2>
            <div id="loginForm">
                <input type="text" id="loginUsername" placeholder="Логин"><input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <button onclick="login()">Войти</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showRegister()">Нет аккаунта? Зарегистрироваться</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function showRegister() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>Регистрация</h2>
            <div id="registerForm">
                <input type="text" id="regFullName" placeholder="ФИО"><input type="text" id="regLogin" placeholder="Логин">
                <input type="password" id="regPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <select id="regRole"><option value="client">Клиент</option><option value="logist">Логист</option><option value="driver">Водитель</option></select>
                <button onclick="register()">Зарегистрироваться</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showAuthForm()">Уже есть аккаунт? Войти</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function register() {
        const fullName = document.getElementById('regFullName')?.value;
        const login = document.getElementById('regLogin')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('regPassword')?.value;
        const role = document.getElementById('regRole')?.value;
        if (!fullName || !login || !password) { showMessage('Заполните все поля', 'error'); return; }
        if (users.find(u => u.login === login)) { showMessage('Пользователь существует', 'error'); return; }
        users.push({ id: Date.now(), fullName, login, password, role });
        saveData();
        showMessage('Регистрация успешна!', 'success');
        showAuthForm();
    }

    function login() {
        const login = document.getElementById('loginUsername')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword')?.value;
        const user = users.find(u => u.login === login && u.password === password);
        if (user) { currentUser = user; localStorage.setItem('cargo_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser)); render(); }
        else { showMessage('Неверный логин или пароль', 'error'); }
    }

    function logout() { currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('cargo_user'); render(); }

    function renderCards() {
        const container = document.getElementById('cardsContainer');
        if (currentUser.role === 'client') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📦 Заказать перевозку</h3><p>Оформление грузоперевозки</p><button onclick="showOrderForm()">Оформить</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📍 Отследить груз</h3><p>Проверка статуса</p><button onclick="trackShipment()">Отследить</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📋 Мои перевозки</h3><p>История заказов</p><button onclick="showMyShipments()">Просмотреть</button></div>`;
        } else if (currentUser.role === 'logist') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📋 Новые заказы</h3><p>Обработка заявок</p><button onclick="showNewOrders()">Обработать</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>🚛 Назначить ТС</h3><p>Распределение транспорта</p><button onclick="assignTransport()">Назначить</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📊 Отчет по перевозкам</h3><p>Статистика</p><button onclick="showReport()">Сформировать</button></div>`;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📍 Мои рейсы</h3><p>Просмотр назначенных рейсов</p><button onclick="showMyRoutes()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>✅ Обновить статус</h3><p>Изменение статуса доставки</p><button onclick="updateStatus()">Обновить</button></div>`;
        }
    }

    function showOrderForm() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Оформление перевозки';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <input id="cargo" placeholder="Описание груза"><input id="weight" placeholder="Вес (кг)">
            <input id="from" placeholder="Откуда"><input id="to" placeholder="Куда">
            <input id="distance" placeholder="Расстояние (км)">
            <button onclick="createShipment()">Рассчитать стоимость</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function createShipment() {
        const cargo = document.getElementById('cargo')?.value;
        const distance = document.getElementById('distance')?.value;
        if (!cargo || !distance) { showMessage('Заполните обязательные поля', 'error'); return; }
        const price = parseInt(distance) * 60;
        shipments.push({ id: Date.now(), cargo, weight: document.getElementById('weight')?.value, from: document.getElementById('from')?.value, to: document.getElementById('to')?.value, distance, price, clientId: currentUser.id, clientName: currentUser.fullName, status: 'Новый', trackingNumber: 'TRK' + Date.now(), createdAt: new Date().toLocaleString() });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage(`Заказ создан! Стоимость: ${price} руб. Трек-номер: TRK${Date.now()}`, 'success');
    }

    function trackShipment() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отслеживание груза';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<input id="trackNum" placeholder="Введите трек-номер"><button onclick="doTrack()">Найти</button><div id="trackResult"></div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function doTrack() {
        const trackNum = document.getElementById('trackNum')?.value;
        const shipment = shipments.find(s => s.trackingNumber === trackNum);
        const resultDiv = document.getElementById('trackResult');
        if (!shipment) { resultDiv.innerHTML = '<p>Груз не найден</p>'; }
        else {
            let statusClass = '';
            if (shipment.status === 'Новый') statusClass = 'status-new';
            else if (shipment.status === 'В пути') statusClass = 'status-transit';
            else statusClass = 'status-delivered';
            resultDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="cargo-card"><strong>Груз: ${shipment.cargo}</strong><br>Маршрут: ${shipment.from} → ${shipment.to}<br>Статус: <span class="track-status ${statusClass}">${shipment.status}</span></div>`;
        }
    }

    function showMyShipments() {
        const myShipments = shipments.filter(s => s.clientId === currentUser.id);
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мои перевозки';
        if (myShipments.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет заказов</p>'; }
        else { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${myShipments.map(s => `<div class="cargo-card"><strong>${s.cargo}</strong><br>${s.from} → ${s.to}<br>Статус: ${s.status}<br>Трек: ${s.trackingNumber}</div>`).join('')}</div>`; }
        openForm();
    }

    function showNewOrders() {
        const newOrders = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'Новый');
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Новые заказы';
        if (newOrders.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет новых заказов</p>'; }
        else { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${newOrders.map(s => `<div class="cargo-card"><strong>${s.cargo}</strong> - ${s.from}→${s.to}<br>Клиент: ${s.clientName}<br>Стоимость: ${s.price} руб<br><button onclick="acceptOrder(${s.id})">✅ Принять в работу</button></div>`).join('')}</div>`; }
        openForm();
    }

    function acceptOrder(id) {
        const shipment = shipments.find(s => s.id === id);
        if (shipment) { shipment.status = 'Принят'; saveData(); showMessage('Заказ принят', 'success'); showNewOrders(); }
    }

    function assignTransport() {
        const acceptedOrders = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'Принят');
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Назначение транспорта';
        if (acceptedOrders.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет заказов для назначения</p>'; }
        else { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select id="orderSelect">${acceptedOrders.map(s => `<option value="${s.id}">${s.cargo} - ${s.from}→${s.to}</option>`).join('')}</select><select id="truckSelect"><option>Фура 20т</option><option>ГАЗель 1.5т</option><option>ЗИЛ 5т</option></select><select id="driverSelect"><option>Водитель Иванов</option><option>Водитель Петров</option></select><button onclick="doAssign()">Назначить</button>`; }
        openForm();
    }

    function doAssign() {
        const orderId = document.getElementById('orderSelect')?.value;
        if (!orderId) { showMessage('Выберите заказ', 'error'); return; }
        const shipment = shipments.find(s => s.id == orderId);
        if (shipment) { shipment.status = 'В пути'; shipment.assignedAt = new Date().toLocaleString(); saveData(); }
        closeForm();
        showMessage('Транспорт назначен', 'success');
    }

    function showReport() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отчет'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="cargo-card">Всего заказов: ${shipments.length}<br>Выполнено: ${shipments.filter(s=>s.status==='Доставлен').length}<br>Выручка: ${shipments.reduce((s,ship)=>s+(ship.price||0),0)} руб</div>`; openForm(); }
    function showMyRoutes() { const myRoutes = shipments.filter(s => s.status === 'В пути'); document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мои рейсы'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = myRoutes.length ? `<div>${myRoutes.map(r=>`<div class="cargo-card">${r.cargo} - ${r.from}→${r.to}<br>Трек: ${r.trackingNumber}</div>`).join('')}</div>` : '<p>Нет рейсов</p>'; openForm(); }
    function updateStatus() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Обновление статуса'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select><option>Выберите рейс</option></select><select><option>В пути</option><option>Доставлен</option></select><button onclick="showMessage('Статус обновлен','success');closeForm()">Обновить</button>`; openForm(); }

    function openForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'block'; }
    function closeForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'none'; }

    if (users.length === 0) {
        users = [{ id: 1, fullName: "Клиент", login: "client", password: "123", role: "client" },
                 { id: 2, fullName: "Логист", login: "logist", password: "123", role: "logist" },
                 { id: 3, fullName: "Водитель", login: "driver", password: "123", role: "driver" }];
        saveData();
    }
    render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

        .toggle-auth { color: #8d6e63; cursor: pointer; margin-top: 15px; display: inline-block; }
        .message {
            padding: 10px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            position: fixed;
            top: 20px;
            right: 20px;
            z-index: 2000;
            display: none;
        }
        .success { background: #d4edda; color: #155724; }
        .error { background: #f8d7da; color: #721c24; }
        .exhibit-card {
            background: #f8f9fa;
            padding: 12px;
            margin-bottom: 10px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            border-left: 3px solid #8d6e63;
        }
        .ticket-price { font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: #e74c3c; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="container">
    <div class="header">
        <div class="logo"><h1>🏛️ Музей</h1><p>Культурное наследие</p></div>
        <div class="auth-buttons" id="authButtons"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="mainContent" class="main-content">
        <div class="welcome-section"><h2>Добро пожаловать, <span id="userName"></span>!</h2><p>Роль: <strong id="userRole"></strong></p></div>
        <div class="cards" id="cardsContainer"></div>
    </div>
    <div id="authContainer" class="auth-container"></div>
</div>
<div class="overlay" id="overlay"></div>
<div class="form-popup" id="formPopup"><h3 id="formTitle">Форма</h3><div id="formContent"></div><button onclick="closeForm()">Закрыть</button></div>

<script>
    let currentUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('museum_user')) || null;
    let users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('museum_users')) || [];
    let tickets = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('museum_tickets')) || [];
    let excursions = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('museum_excursions')) || [];

    const exhibits = [
        { id: 1, name: "Картина 'Мона Лиза'", period: "Ренессанс", hall: 1 },
        { id: 2, name: "Скульптура 'Давид'", period: "Ренессанс", hall: 2 },
        { id: 3, name: "Египетская мумия", period: "Древний Египет", hall: 3 },
        { id: 4, name: "Древнегреческая ваза", period: "Античность", hall: 4 }
    ];

    function saveData() {
        localStorage.setItem('museum_users', JSON.stringify(users));
        localStorage.setItem('museum_tickets', JSON.stringify(tickets));
        localStorage.setItem('museum_excursions', JSON.stringify(excursions));
    }

    function showMessage(text, type) {
        let msg = document.createElement('div');
        msg.className = `message ${type}`;
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
        document.body.appendChild(msg);
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 3000);
    }

    function render() {
        const authContainer = document.getElementById('authContainer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('mainContent');
        const authButtons = document.getElementById('authButtons');
        if (currentUser) {
            authContainer.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('userName').textContent = currentUser.fullName || currentUser.login;
            document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = currentUser.role === 'visitor' ? 'Посетитель' : (currentUser.role === 'guide' ? 'Гид' : 'Администратор');
            authButtons.innerHTML = `<button class="logout-btn" onclick="logout()">Выйти</button>`;
            renderCards();
        } else {
            authContainer.style.display = 'block';
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            authButtons.innerHTML = '';
            showAuthForm();
        }
    }

    function showAuthForm() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>🏛️ Музей</h2>
            <div id="loginForm">
                <input type="text" id="loginUsername" placeholder="Логин"><input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <button onclick="login()">Войти</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showRegister()">Нет аккаунта? Зарегистрироваться</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function showRegister() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>Регистрация</h2>
            <div id="registerForm">
                <input type="text" id="regFullName" placeholder="ФИО"><input type="text" id="regLogin" placeholder="Логин">
                <input type="password" id="regPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <select id="regRole"><option value="visitor">Посетитель</option><option value="guide">Гид</option><option value="admin">Администратор</option></select>
                <button onclick="register()">Зарегистрироваться</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showAuthForm()">Уже есть аккаунт? Войти</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function register() {
        const fullName = document.getElementById('regFullName')?.value;
        const login = document.getElementById('regLogin')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('regPassword')?.value;
        const role = document.getElementById('regRole')?.value;
        if (!fullName || !login || !password) { showMessage('Заполните все поля', 'error'); return; }
        if (users.find(u => u.login === login)) { showMessage('Пользователь существует', 'error'); return; }
        users.push({ id: Date.now(), fullName, login, password, role });
        saveData();
        showMessage('Регистрация успешна!', 'success');
        showAuthForm();
    }

    function login() {
        const login = document.getElementById('loginUsername')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword')?.value;
        const user = users.find(u => u.login === login && u.password === password);
        if (user) { currentUser = user; localStorage.setItem('museum_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser)); render(); }
        else { showMessage('Неверный логин или пароль', 'error'); }
    }

    function logout() { currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('museum_user'); render(); }

    function renderCards() {
        const container = document.getElementById('cardsContainer');
        if (currentUser.role === 'visitor') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>🎫 Купить билет</h3><p>Приобретите входной билет</p><button onclick="buyTicket()">Купить</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>🗿 Экспонаты</h3><p>Просмотр коллекции музея</p><button onclick="viewExhibits()">Смотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>🚶 Запись на экскурсию</h3><p>Экскурсия с гидом</p><button onclick="bookExcursion()">Записаться</button></div>`;
        } else if (currentUser.role === 'guide') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📋 Мои экскурсии</h3><p>Расписание экскурсий</p><button onclick="showGuideExcursions()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>👥 Группы</h3><p>Список записавшихся</p><button onclick="showGroups()">Смотреть</button></div>`;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>📅 Управление расписанием</h3><p>Создание экскурсий</p><button onclick="manageSchedule()">Управлять</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📊 Отчет по посещаемости</h3><p>Статистика музея</p><button onclick="showReport()">Сформировать</button></div>`;
        }
    }

    function buyTicket() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Покупка билета';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <select id="ticketType">
                <option value="adult">Взрослый - 500 руб</option>
                <option value="student">Студенческий - 300 руб</option>
                <option value="child">Детский - 200 руб</option>
            </select>
            <input type="date" id="visitDate">
            <button onclick="purchaseTicket()">Оплатить</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function purchaseTicket() {
        const type = document.getElementById('ticketType')?.value;
        const date = document.getElementById('visitDate')?.value;
        if (!date) { showMessage('Выберите дату', 'error'); return; }
        let price = type === 'adult' ? 500 : (type === 'student' ? 300 : 200);
        tickets.push({ id: Date.now(), userId: currentUser.id, userName: currentUser.fullName, type, price, date, qrCode: 'TICKET' + Date.now() });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage(`Билет приобретен! QR-код: TICKET${Date.now()}`, 'success');
    }

    function viewExhibits() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Экспонаты музея';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${exhibits.map(e => `<div class="exhibit-card"><strong>${e.name}</strong><br>Период: ${e.period}<br>Зал: ${e.hall}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function bookExcursion() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Запись на экскурсию';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `
            <select id="excursionSelect">
                <option>Обзорная экскурсия - 11:00</option>
                <option>Шедевры живописи - 14:00</option>
                <option>Древний мир - 16:00</option>
            </select>
            <input type="date" id="excursionDate">
            <button onclick="submitExcursion()">Записаться</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function submitExcursion() {
        const excursion = document.getElementById('excursionSelect')?.value;
        const date = document.getElementById('excursionDate')?.value;
        if (!date) { showMessage('Выберите дату', 'error'); return; }
        excursions.push({ id: Date.now(), userId: currentUser.id, userName: currentUser.fullName, excursionName: excursion, date, status: 'Записан' });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage('Вы записаны на экскурсию', 'success');
    }

    function showGuideExcursions() {
        const guideExcursions = excursions.filter(e => e.status === 'Записан');
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Мои экскурсии';
        if (guideExcursions.length === 0) { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<p>Нет записей</p>'; }
        else { document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${guideExcursions.map(e => `<div class="exhibit-card">${e.excursionName}<br>${e.date}<br>Участник: ${e.userName}</div>`).join('')}</div>`; }
        openForm();
    }

    function showGroups() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Группы'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = '<div class="exhibit-card">Обзорная экскурсия: 5 человек<br>Живопись: 3 человека</div>'; openForm(); }
    function manageSchedule() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Управление'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<input placeholder="Название экскурсии"><input type="date"><input type="time"><button onclick="showMessage('Экскурсия добавлена','success');closeForm()">Добавить</button>`; openForm(); }
    function showReport() { document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отчет'; document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="exhibit-card">Посетителей за месяц: 1250<br>Выручка: 450 000 руб</div>`; openForm(); }

    function openForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'block'; }
    function closeForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'none'; }

    if (users.length === 0) {
        users = [{ id: 1, fullName: "Посетитель", login: "visitor", password: "123", role: "visitor" },
                 { id: 2, fullName: "Гид", login: "guide", password: "123", role: "guide" },
                 { id: 3, fullName: "Админ", login: "admin", password: "123", role: "admin" }];
        saveData();
    }
    render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
<div class="container">

</div>
<div class="overlay" id="overlay"></div>
<div class="form-popup" id="formPopup"><h3 id="formTitle">Форма</h3><div id="formContent"></div><button onclick="closeForm()">Закрыть</button></div>

<script>
    let currentUser = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('farm_user')) || null;
    let users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('farm_users')) || [];
    let animals = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('farm_animals')) || [];
    let crops = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('farm_crops')) || [];
    let products = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('farm_products')) || [];

    function saveData() {
        localStorage.setItem('farm_users', JSON.stringify(users));
        localStorage.setItem('farm_animals', JSON.stringify(animals));
        localStorage.setItem('farm_crops', JSON.stringify(crops));
        localStorage.setItem('farm_products', JSON.stringify(products));
    }

    function showMessage(text, type) {
        let msg = document.createElement('div');
        msg.className = `message ${type}`;
        msg.textContent = text;
        msg.style.display = 'block';
        document.body.appendChild(msg);
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 3000);
    }

    function render() {
        const authContainer = document.getElementById('authContainer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('mainContent');
        const authButtons = document.getElementById('authButtons');
        if (currentUser) {
            authContainer.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('userName').textContent = currentUser.fullName || currentUser.login;
            document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = currentUser.role === 'agronomist' ? 'Агроном' : (currentUser.role === 'zootechnician' ? 'Зоотехник' : 'Бухгалтер');
            authButtons.innerHTML = `<button class="logout-btn" onclick="logout()">Выйти</button>`;
            renderCards();
        } else {
            authContainer.style.display = 'block';
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            authButtons.innerHTML = '';
            showAuthForm();
        }
    }

    function showAuthForm() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>🌾 Фермерское хозяйство</h2>
            <div id="loginForm">
                <input type="text" id="loginUsername" placeholder="Логин"><input type="password" id="loginPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <button onclick="login()">Войти</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showRegister()">Нет аккаунта? Зарегистрироваться</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function showRegister() {
        document.getElementById('authContainer').innerHTML = `
            <h2>Регистрация</h2>
            <div id="registerForm">
                <input type="text" id="regFullName" placeholder="ФИО"><input type="text" id="regLogin" placeholder="Логин">
                <input type="password" id="regPassword" placeholder="Пароль">
                <select id="regRole"><option value="agronomist">Агроном</option><option value="zootechnician">Зоотехник</option><option value="accountant">Бухгалтер</option></select>
                <button onclick="register()">Зарегистрироваться</button>
                <div class="toggle-auth" onclick="showAuthForm()">Уже есть аккаунт? Войти</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    function register() {
        const fullName = document.getElementById('regFullName')?.value;
        const login = document.getElementById('regLogin')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('regPassword')?.value;
        const role = document.getElementById('regRole')?.value;
        if (!fullName || !login || !password) { showMessage('Заполните все поля', 'error'); return; }
        if (users.find(u => u.login === login)) { showMessage('Пользователь существует', 'error'); return; }
        users.push({ id: Date.now(), fullName, login, password, role });
        saveData();
        showMessage('Регистрация успешна!', 'success');
        showAuthForm();
    }

    function login() {
        const login = document.getElementById('loginUsername')?.value;
        const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword')?.value;
        const user = users.find(u => u.login === login && u.password === password);
        if (user) { currentUser = user; localStorage.setItem('farm_user', JSON.stringify(currentUser)); render(); }
        else { showMessage('Неверный логин или пароль', 'error'); }
    }

    function logout() { currentUser = null; localStorage.removeItem('farm_user'); render(); }

    if (animals.length === 0) {
        animals = [
            { id: 1, type: "Корова", breed: "Голштинская", count: 50, milk: "25 л/день" },
            { id: 2, type: "Свинья", breed: "Ландрас", count: 120, weight: "100 кг" }
        ];
        crops = [
            { id: 1, name: "Пшеница", area: 50, planted: "10.04", harvest: "август", yield: "40 ц/га" },
            { id: 2, name: "Кукуруза", area: 30, planted: "15.05", harvest: "сентябрь", yield: "60 ц/га" }
        ];
        saveData();
    }

    function renderCards() {
        const container = document.getElementById('cardsContainer');
        if (currentUser.role === 'agronomist') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>🌱 Посевные культуры</h3><p>Управление посевами</p><button onclick="showCrops()">Управлять</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📊 Урожайность</h3><p>Отчет по урожаю</p><button onclick="showYield()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>➕ Добавить культуру</h3><p>Расширение посевных</p><button onclick="addCropForm()">Добавить</button></div>`;
        } else if (currentUser.role === 'zootechnician') {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>🐄 Поголовье скота</h3><p>Управление животными</p><button onclick="showAnimals()">Просмотреть</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>💉 Вакцинация</h3><p>Ветеринарные мероприятия</p><button onclick="showVaccination()">Провести</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>➕ Добавить животное</h3><p>Пополнение стада</p><button onclick="addAnimalForm()">Добавить</button></div>`;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card"><h3>💰 Себестоимость</h3><p>Расчет затрат</p><button onclick="showCost()">Рассчитать</button></div>
                <div class="card"><h3>📊 Отчетность</h3><p>Налоговая отчетность</p><button onclick="showTaxReport()">Сформировать</button></div>`;
        }
    }

    function showCrops() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Посевные культуры';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${crops.map(c => `<div class="crop-card"><strong>${c.name}</strong><br>Площадь: ${c.area} га<br>Посев: ${c.planted}<br>Урожайность: ${c.yield}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function showYield() {
        const totalYield = crops.reduce((s, c) => s + (parseInt(c.area) * 40), 0);
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Отчет по урожайности';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="crop-card">Общий сбор зерна: ${totalYield} ц<br>Пшеница: 2000 ц<br>Кукуруза: 1800 ц</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function addCropForm() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Добавление культуры';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<input id="cropName" placeholder="Название"><input id="area" placeholder="Площадь (га)"><input id="planted" placeholder="Дата посева"><button onclick="addCrop()">Добавить</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function addCrop() {
        const name = document.getElementById('cropName')?.value;
        if (!name) { showMessage('Введите название', 'error'); return; }
        crops.push({ id: Date.now(), name, area: document.getElementById('area')?.value, planted: document.getElementById('planted')?.value, harvest: "осень", yield: "30 ц/га" });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage('Культура добавлена', 'success');
    }

    function showAnimals() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Поголовье скота';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div>${animals.map(a => `<div class="animal-card"><strong>${a.type}</strong> (${a.breed})<br>Количество: ${a.count}<br>${a.milk ? 'Надой: ' + a.milk : 'Вес: ' + a.weight}</div>`).join('')}</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function showVaccination() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Вакцинация';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select><option>Коровы</option><option>Свиньи</option></select><input type="date"><button onclick="showMessage('Вакцинация проведена','success');closeForm()">Провести</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function addAnimalForm() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Добавление животного';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<select id="animalType"><option>Корова</option><option>Свинья</option><option>Овца</option></select><input id="breed" placeholder="Порода"><input id="count" placeholder="Количество"><button onclick="addAnimal()">Добавить</button>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function addAnimal() {
        const type = document.getElementById('animalType')?.value;
        const count = document.getElementById('count')?.value;
        if (!type || !count) { showMessage('Заполните поля', 'error'); return; }
        animals.push({ id: Date.now(), type, breed: document.getElementById('breed')?.value, count: parseInt(count), milk: type === 'Корова' ? "20 л/день" : null, weight: type !== 'Корова' ? "80 кг" : null });
        saveData();
        closeForm();
        showMessage('Животные добавлены', 'success');
    }

    function showCost() {
        const totalCost = 1500000;
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Себестоимость продукции';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="animal-card">Затраты на корма: 500 000 руб<br>Зарплата: 400 000 руб<br>Ветеринария: 100 000 руб<br><strong>Итого: ${totalCost.toLocaleString()} руб</strong></div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function showTaxReport() {
        document.getElementById('formTitle').textContent = 'Налоговая отчетность';
        document.getElementById('formContent').innerHTML = `<div class="animal-card">ЕСХН: 150 000 руб<br>Срок уплаты: 25.10.2024</div>`;
        openForm();
    }

    function openForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'block'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'block'; }
    function closeForm() { document.getElementById('formPopup').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display = 'none'; }

    if (users.length === 0) {
        users = [{ id: 1, fullName: "Агроном", login: "agro", password: "123", role: "agronomist" },
                 { id: 2, fullName: "Зоотехник", login: "zoo", password: "123", role: "zootechnician" },
                 { id: 3, fullName: "Бухгалтер", login: "accountant", password: "123", role: "accountant" }];
        saveData();
    }
    render();
</script>
</body>
</html>

Вариант 21: Школа иностранных языков
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="ru">

    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Школа иностранных языков - Обучение</title>
    <style>
        * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }
        body {
            font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #3498db 0%, #2980b9 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
            padding: 20px;
        }
        .container {
            max-width: 1200px;
            width: 100%;
            background: white;
            border-radius: 20px;
            overflow: hidden;

        }
        .header {
            background: #2980b9;
            color: white;
            padding: 20px 30px;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .logo h1 { font-size: 1.5rem; }
        .auth-buttons button {
            background: #e74c3c;

        .auth-buttons .logout-btn { background: #7f8c8d; }

        .cards {
            display: grid;
            grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(280px, 1fr));
            gap: 20px;
            margin-top: 20px;
        }
        .card {
            background: #f8f9fa;
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 15px;
            border-left: 4px solid #3498db;
        }
        .card h3 { color: #2980b9; margin-bottom: 15px; }
        .card button {
            background: #3498db;
            color: white;

            padding: 8px 15px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .form-popup {
            display: none;

            top: 50%;

            background: white;
            padding: 30px;
            border-radius: 15px;
            width: 450px;
            max-height: 80vh;
            overflow-y: auto;
            z-index: 1000;
        }
        .form-popup input, .form-popup select, .form-popup textarea {
            width: 100%;

            border: 1px solid #ddd;

        }
        .form-popup button {

            border: none;
            padding: 10px;
            width: 100%;
            border-radius: 5px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        .overlay {
            display: none;
            position: fixed;
            top: 0;
            left: 0;
            width: 100%;
